        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2143921091" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14249138949881919986"><u>5 THE PAST WILL NOT FORGET ME ★'s</u><br/><br/><i>“I cannot let the broken girl inside of me inhale all that I've become. I cannot revert back to another version of myself. I will not shatter, not again, in the wake of an emotional earthquake.”</i><br/><br/><i>“The destruction of the world didn’t happen overnight, and neither will saving it.”</i> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521269490i/25226814._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Holy. Fucking. Shit.</b> That was insane! I can't even begin to process what the hell I'm feeling, because there are way, way, way, to many emotions going through me at the moment. My mind is r</span>
  <span id="freeText14249138949881919986" style="display:none"><u>5 THE PAST WILL NOT FORGET ME ★'s</u><br><br><i>“I cannot let the broken girl inside of me inhale all that I've become. I cannot revert back to another version of myself. I will not shatter, not again, in the wake of an emotional earthquake.”</i><br><br><i>“The destruction of the world didn’t happen overnight, and neither will saving it.”</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521269490i/25226814._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Holy. Fucking. Shit.</b> That was insane! I can't even begin to process what the hell I'm feeling, because there are way, way, way, to many emotions going through me at the moment. My mind is reeling at everything that has just conspired. My strongest emotion throughout reading 'Restore Me' was a deep sadness. Heartache. It was like having a bowling ball sitting on my chest the whole time and I couldn't breathe. It put tears in my eyes in the second chapter...<b>THE SECOND DAMN CHAPTER!!!</b> Witch is in Warner's POV. So now you understand exactly how long I've had this weight on my chest and it's still there. You won't just cry, you will also laugh and smile and swoon (Over Warner). 'Restore Me' was so unbelievably unbearably wonderfully Painful! My heart broke piece by piece until finally, what was left of it just shattered and I don't know how to put it back together. I am equal parts happy and pissed off, but in a good way, if that makes any sense. I devoured this in <b>ONE</b> day! It was so captivating, it had me at the edge of my seat. The world, the plot, the writing and the characters are everything. The best way to describe what happens is this- One bad thing happens after another, revelation after revelation, about the Reestablishment, things about Juliette and Warner's past. I'm still in shock after that ending!! I have no idea how in the hell Tahereh Mafi expects us to wait a <b>WHOLE YEAR</b> to read the next book. When I'm already dying to know what happens! This wait is gonna be the death of me :(<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521269490i/25226814._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>“This, I think, is the way to die.<br>I could drown in this moment and I’d never regret it. I could catch fire from this kiss and happily turn to ash. I could live here, die here, right here, against his hips, his lips. In the emotion in his eyes as he sinks into me, his heartbeats indistinguishable from mine.<br>This. Forever. This.” <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521270776ra/25226862.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521269490i/25226814._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>“It hits me with a painful force, the reminder. Of just how much I love her. God, I love all of her. Her impossibilities, her exasperations. I love how gentle she is with me when we’re alone. How soft and kind she can be in our quiet moments. How she never hesitates to defend me.<br>I love her.” <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521269141ra/25226795.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>*Omg! That cover is absolutely freaking stunning!!!*</b></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983286834" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4385302615937790023"><b>*****UPDATE OCTOBER 6TH COVER REVEAL****</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507247318i/24095547._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I love it! I don't think it's <b>MY</b> Warner's eye? I love that it matches perfectly the rest of the covers of the previous books!<br/><br/>I always imagine <b>my man</b> Warner's eye more masculine.<br/><br/>Are you new to the Shatter me series? I have to tell you that the series start in the young adult side and by book 3 we have more sex. Not graphic, mostly sensual imagery, nothing like the jump between Throne of glass book 1 (upper young adult) to almost porn XXX content that you'll</span>
  <span id="freeText4385302615937790023" style="display:none"><b>*****UPDATE OCTOBER 6TH COVER REVEAL****</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507247318i/24095547._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I love it! I don't think it's <b>MY</b> Warner's eye? I love that it matches perfectly the rest of the covers of the previous books!<br><br>I always imagine <b>my man</b> Warner's eye more masculine.<br><br>Are you new to the Shatter me series? I have to tell you that the series start in the young adult side and by book 3 we have more sex. Not graphic, mostly sensual imagery, nothing like the jump between Throne of glass book 1 (upper young adult) to almost porn XXX content that you'll find in Empire of storms book 5 of TOG (new adult/adult). But the financial success of this approach, starting as young adult and then change to new adult/erotica as the series progress, might become a trend, specially in books from the big publishing houses. Using some booktubers and sites like Kirkus reviews and Common sense media to hide the problematic content of a book is also common practice of the big publishing houses.<br><br>Either way I think it's time for <b>honest</b> reviewers, booktubers and librarians, to add information of sexual content and not try to cover it up as it has been the case with the erotic content of Sarah J Maas books. My friends read YA because they think , wrongly, that it's a sexless genre. We need this information of the content we'll find in a book to make informed decisions. I wonder how many parents really know about this tendency of market New adult/adult books with erotic content as safe for underage readers. Either way If I were you I wouldn't give certain series as a gift to underage readers now that Christmas season is approaching.<br><br><br>Don't take me wrong. I love the idea of Warner sexy times if that was the case. This book might actually sell more if the Publishers advertise as Warner sexy times! This is 2017 and new adult is a very respectable genre. Just add warnings in the blurb and make sure the reviewers mention this. Don't make reviewers and booktubers hide this information.<br><br>Is there an honest goodreads librarian reading this? Could you please add sexual content disclaimers in the Goodreads blurbs of A COURT OF MIST AND FURY, Ignite me and Empire of storms ?<br><br><br><br><br>Original prereading thoughts:<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>This has to be my most anticipated book of 2018! I just can't wait. <br><br><br>I just hope Mafi doesn't take the A court of mist and fury route and starts to write erotic scenes in a book marketed as Young adult. Ignite me was pretty much new adult, and I like that, but I'm tired of publishers and authors shoving sex-scenes down young readers throats without proper warnings. We have enough authors selling erotica to children like Elle Kennedy and Sarah J Maas without Mafi joining the crowd.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1982985690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6348908429939268304"><b>April 26th, 2017:</b><br/><br/>I'm torn between 'GIVE IT TO ME NOW' and 'please, don't ruin my ship, my precious otp...'<br/>Also I liked how Ignite Me ended, soooooooo I guess we'll see *keeps all the fingers crossed*<br/><br/><b>March 17th, 2018:</b><br/><br/><i>“All of you kids,” he says, shaking his head. “You suffer too much. You have these horrible, tragic histories. Volatile personalities. I've always wanted to help,” he says. “I've always wanted to fix that. Make this world a better place for you kids.”</i><br/><br/>I cannot believe I had to wait fo</span>
  <span id="freeText6348908429939268304" style="display:none"><b>April 26th, 2017:</b><br /><br />I'm torn between 'GIVE IT TO ME NOW' and 'please, don't ruin my ship, my precious otp...'<br />Also I liked how Ignite Me ended, soooooooo I guess we'll see *keeps all the fingers crossed*<br /><br /><b>March 17th, 2018:</b><br /><br /><i>“All of you kids,” he says, shaking his head. “You suffer too much. You have these horrible, tragic histories. Volatile personalities. I've always wanted to help,” he says. “I've always wanted to fix that. Make this world a better place for you kids.”</i><br /><br />I cannot believe I had to wait for three years to read this book. And now it’s done, and we have to wait another full year to know what happens next. This is a new kind of torture. Well done, Tahereh. Well done.<br /><br />I was one of those who thought the end of <i>Ignite Me</i> was perfect. I genuinely liked how the story finished, we didn’t know exactly what Juliette and Warner would have to go through, but we had put our hope in them. Well, even my ‘I loved Ignite Me’s end’ ass loved this book. I see how it’s not for everybody, because true, it’s a very slow book, nothing really happens, but for a first book in this new trilogy? It’s perfect. It answers all the questions I had about Juliette’s past and it’s realistic? Like, I would have found it weird if Juliette had been able to be this perfect Supreme Commander even though she’s fucking new to this world.<br /><br />This book is more about Juliette and Warner confronting their past, thinking about what’s going to happen next now that they’re in power. What comes next? What should they do? Who should they trust? And we finally learn more about this world, about why the Reestablishment was created in the first place, how it was created, who is at its head …. all these questions I had are starting to get answered.<br /><br />This book destroyed my soul. I hurt so much throughout this book but in a way I’m hopeful for what’s to come in the next book. I trust Tahereh.<br /><br /><b>May 8th, 2020:</b><br /><br />look at how casually I'm bumping this book from 4.75 to 5 stars:)))))))))) this reread destroyed everything I had in me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6348908429939268304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1983173875" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983173875" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1983173875?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983173875" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18095887668911796577"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520532050ra/25182731.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> „Were you happy <br/>Were you sad <br/>Were you scared <br/>Were you mad the first time you screamed? <br/>Were you fighting for your life <br/>your decency <br/>your dignity <br/>your humanity <br/>When someone touches you now, do you scream? <br/>When someone smiles at you now, do you smile back? <br/>Did he tell you not to scream did he hit you when you cried? <br/>Did he have one nose two eyes two lips two cheeks two ears two eyebrows. <br/>Was he one human who looked just like you. Color your personality. <br/>Shapes and sizes are variety. <br/>Your heart is</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18095887668911796577" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520532050ra/25182731.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> „Were you happy <br>Were you sad <br>Were you scared <br>Were you mad the first time you screamed? <br>Were you fighting for your life <br>your decency <br>your dignity <br>your humanity <br>When someone touches you now, do you scream? <br>When someone smiles at you now, do you smile back? <br>Did he tell you not to scream did he hit you when you cried? <br>Did he have one nose two eyes two lips two cheeks two ears two eyebrows. <br>Was he one human who looked just like you. Color your personality. <br>Shapes and sizes are variety. <br>Your heart is an anomaly. <br>Your actions are the only traces you leave behind.“ </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>First of all: WHAT THE HELL?? HOW COULD MAFI END THID BOOK WITH SUCH A DEVASTATING CLIFF HANGER?! <br>Oh my god this book was so addictive, so good, so heartbreaking and absolutely brutal. <br>I’ll probably need to recover until the next book comes out. <br>Oh, and I need to try to piece my heart back together. <br>How long do we need to wait for the next book? I feel like it’s already been ages (it came out two days ago and I finished it like twenty seconds ago, but still... feels like an eternity). <br>I know some of you are a little bit unsure about the whole fourth book thing, but I was really happy diving into this world and meeting all my favorite characters again. <br>If you were skeptical about Juliet’s role as a ruler, you get a few answers in this book. <br>Also, we get a few new characters, lots of drama and action and Juliet is finally an absolute badass. <br>Oh, and don’t forget Warner. I loved him in the first/second/third book and nothing changed in the fourth book. <br>He didn’t have a nice fluffy childhood with loving parents and real friends. But we get to know a lot about his past and that makes me really happy. <br>All in all I’m really happy that I read this book, because I was finally able to see their story continue. And there were so many plot twists! Holy sh**! <br>I can’t wait for the next two books to come. <br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Finally Juliet grew up to be an adult. Not full mode adult, but like a little bit more mature than in the previous books. <br>She’s still a teenager, she still makes mistakes, but that’s absolutely normal. If someone would write a perfect, super intelligent main character with no flaws I would probably throw this book out of the window. <br>But this... she’s not perfect and that makes her so much more relatable. <br>Of course Warner played a big role in this book. He’s still this supportive, handsome partner, but we get to see that Warner had an even more horrible childhood than we all assumed. <br>We get to see a weaker part of him we never noticed before. <br>And it made him even more lovable. ♥️<br>My dream-best-friend Kenji aka handsome boy aka funniest guy on the planet has a strong role in this book. He’s the perfect best friend we all want to have and I absolute love him.<br>Also we have a few new characters, that are actually pretty fascinating and cool, so I can’t wait for the other books so we can meet them a little bit more. <br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>We get to see how the Reestablishment actually separated the whole world and how they’re accomplished their strong hold on the world and power. <br>It was super interesting to see the whole mechanism, history and people. <br>Also we have gay, transsexual and all types of different people. I loved it! Finally Tahereh did some refreshing changes and put in some interesting new characters (even though we just met them some short time). <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Oh my god. <br>Drama. There’s drama everywhere. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520531684ra/25182713.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In the beginning of this book I was super super happy only to get my heart broke into a thousand pieces and then Tahereh actually burned my heart down. <br>Did it kill me? Probably. <br>Was it heartbreaking? Definitely. <br>Will I read it again only to die a few times more? Absolutely. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449086549ra/17231751.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Oh, Tahereh. You freakin genius. <br>Your writing is everything and I love it so much. <br>Warner’s POV was exactly what I wanted and didn’t know I needed. Really looking into his mind and seeing all this thoughts and emotions was beautiful. <br>Oh my god, I loved it. <br>They were excerpts out of Juliet’s journal from book two and I was a little bit skeptical about it, but then a friend said, that with the excerpts you can actually see that Juliet’s past comes hunting her down. <br>They were scenes I will never forget and conversations I loved.<br><br>____________________________________________________<br><br>Me: <i> “Hello? Yeah, it’s Jessi. I can’t come to work today, Restore me came out.” </i><br><br>Also me: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482417625ra/21515380.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Btw. Three pages in and I’m (again) head over heels in love with Warner. ♥️</span>

<div id="review_1983097713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983097713" />
    <a title="Candace Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33995641-candace-robinson"><img alt="Candace Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530157383p2/33995641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1983097713?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace Robinson" href="/user/show/33995641-candace-robinson">Candace Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983097713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8613188259868178210">Okay, so I was super duper scared to go into this one since Shatter Me is my favorite series ever. But of course I was intrigued. Especially when I found out it was going to be told in two perspectives, and one of those being Warner!<br/><br/>I loved that this book was dark, depressing, and addicting. I already knew going in, since it was going to be book number 4 and there are going to be six total, that there were going to be things that would piss me off and drive me crazy. And boy did they ever!<br/><br/>I’m al</span>
  <span id="freeText8613188259868178210" style="display:none">Okay, so I was super duper scared to go into this one since Shatter Me is my favorite series ever. But of course I was intrigued. Especially when I found out it was going to be told in two perspectives, and one of those being Warner!<br /><br />I loved that this book was dark, depressing, and addicting. I already knew going in, since it was going to be book number 4 and there are going to be six total, that there were going to be things that would piss me off and drive me crazy. And boy did they ever!<br /><br />I’m also so glad that Mafi writes these teens like teens and not like their forty. Because when I was a teen I was an idiot and made dumb choices—I’m pretty sure I still do now! Also, the chemistry between Juliette and Warner was just as good as before. Whether they are happy or arguing it’s all ignited!<br /><br />Just don’t go into book four expecting all sunshine and rainbows! I absolutely loved it! And am aching for the next book because holy smokes, that cliffhanger!<br /><br />Review on my blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://literarydust.wordpress.com/2018/03/14/review-restore-me/">https://literarydust.wordpress.com/20...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8613188259868178210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2089384918" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2089384918" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2089384918?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2089384918" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6377489260553715788"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520362771ra/25171915.gif' width='450' height='281' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Going into this book was a weird experience for me. When this trilogy <i>ended</i> back in 2014 it ended abruptly and with no epilogue. No even a hint of what may happen after Juliette sized control over Sector 45 and one of my issues with the trilogy was its lack of world building -so much wasted potential. <br/><br/>But when the news hit and suddenly we were getting more books? Boy, was I excited. Yes! This is one of the few “finished” series that deserved more books. I was thrilled. Hesitating but thrilled.<br/><br/>As</span>
  <span id="freeText6377489260553715788" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520362771ra/25171915.gif" width="450" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Going into this book was a weird experience for me. When this trilogy <i>ended</i> back in 2014 it ended abruptly and with no epilogue. No even a hint of what may happen after Juliette sized control over Sector 45 and one of my issues with the trilogy was its lack of world building -so much wasted potential. <br><br>But when the news hit and suddenly we were getting more books? Boy, was I excited. Yes! This is one of the few “finished” series that deserved more books. I was thrilled. Hesitating but thrilled.<br><br>As a matter of fact, I did not what to expect from Tahereh. After Ignite Me was released I didn’t follow on her other projects, leaving me with only 2014 Tahereh as reference but I was pleasantly surprised finding joy in this book. I was excited, but I was keeping my expectations low and what I found was a very logical book that followed right after the events in Ignite Me.<br><br>Everything that happened in Restore Me was a consequence of all that went down in the previous books -Juliette doubting herself and feeling lost at power, Warnette at risk (they were like <b>really together for only about few chapters back in Ignite Me before shit hit the fan. </b>), Castle and his somewhat shady ways, oh and the rest of the world getting ready to demolish them because <i>of course</i> that was going to happen. So, this book felt very organic.<br><br>Juliette was, as always, a pleasure to read. She was a display of emotions and consequences and even though some will perceive her in this book as if she fell back into Shatter Me Juliette, I liked that. Like I said, it was logical. She just overthrew a tyrant and got a continent with very little education and a volatile set of powers. Her fears and concerns made sense. Just like Warner.<br><br>I wanted to be upset and blame him as much as he was blaming himself, but I couldn’t. He was also new in this relationship and both him and Juliette came with a lot of emotional baggage and with all these changes… yeah, I get why he was behaving like that even though it was a mistake<br><br>This whole revolution took a toll on all the characters and it shows. <br><br>The secrets that were revealed, some of them I didn’t see coming and got me all giggly and excited. It was a cool experience. It was like a happy version of 2014 me emerging from within me to say hi. I liked the twists very much.<br><br>I also liked the new characters a lot. I want to read more about them and learn more about the way The Reestablishment has, not only shaped them into who they are now but also the lands they come from.<br><br>Overall it was a very solid comeback and I couldn’t be more excited for what’s next.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6377489260553715788" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1984606617?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Janett" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Janett" href="/user/show/60726746-janett">Janett</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/60726746-janett?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/60726746-janett?shelf=2018-read">2018-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/60726746-janett?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1984606617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9269977774519295155"><b>5 unholy stars! <br/><br/>Re-read July 2018</b><br/><br/>Okay, I had to read this again because it was just too amazing the first time. But the second time around was even better! The PAIN of it all! I seriously can't wait to see where this story takes us next! <br/><br/>I am keeping my rating at a solid 5 stars! <br/><br/>Tahereh's writing keeps surging especially when she writes Warner's character. The words, the sentence structures... the DEPTH! It blows me away. <br/><br/>I will add that I've been intrigued by Warner listening to <b>
  <i>"Like A Rol</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText9269977774519295155" style="display:none"><b>5 unholy stars! <br><br>Re-read July 2018</b><br><br>Okay, I had to read this again because it was just too amazing the first time. But the second time around was even better! The PAIN of it all! I seriously can't wait to see where this story takes us next! <br><br>I am keeping my rating at a solid 5 stars! <br><br>Tahereh's writing keeps surging especially when she writes Warner's character. The words, the sentence structures... the DEPTH! It blows me away. <br><br>I will add that I've been intrigued by Warner listening to <b>
  <i>"Like A Rolling Stone"</i>
</b> by Bob Dylan. The message is so dark and I can totally feel the pain of loss and instability he must've been feeling. HOW DID I MISS THIS BEFORE?!!<br><br>This is the beauty of reading and taking time to digest a story and its characters. You really get the essence of who they are. <br><br>My Warner just continues to break my heart 💔<br><br><i>How does it feel, how does it feel?<br>To be on you own, with no direction home<br>Like a complete unknown, like a rolling stone</i><br><br>__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*<br><br>No! No! NOOOOO! AAAAACK!!! WTH did I just read in this book?!<br><br>😭😢😭<br><br>My mind and poor broken heart need time to process this... this IS craaaaazy!!!<br><br><b>SCROLL DOWN FOR MY REVIEW!<br><br>__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*__*_*</b><br><br><br><b>ONE OF MY DREAMS CAME TRUE LAST NIGHT!!!<br><br>I met Tahereh, the mother of my all-time sexy, dreamboat, book boyfriend!<br><br>I am officially freaking dead!!!!<br><br>_**__**__**__**__**__**__**__**__**__**_<br><br>Tahereh posted this on Twitter!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1518361889p8/3671754.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I. AM. SPEECHLESS!!!<br><br>Nothing, NOTHING could've prepared me…EVER for the twist this book took!!!<br><br>AAAARRRRGGGGHHHHH!!!!<br><br>I have waited 3 insufferable years wishing for just one more book…just a little taste of what happened after the end of “<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13188676.Ignite_Me__Shatter_Me___3_" title="Ignite Me (Shatter Me, #3) by Tahereh Mafi" rel="nofollow noopener">Ignite Me</a>”<br><br>I want to kiss Tahereh Mafi for gifting us with “<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34992929.Restore_Me__Shatter_Me___4_" title="Restore Me (Shatter Me, #4) by Tahereh Mafi" rel="nofollow noopener">Restore Me</a>”, book 4 in her awesome <i>“Shatter Me”</i> series.<br><br>I was all smiles and had so many warm fuzzies blooming in my chest as my beloved characters greeted me with wide, open arms like old friends welcoming me back home after a long vacation. <br><br>By chapter 2 I was a TOTAL WRECK!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472169306ra/20160826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My body was shaking, my mind spinning, my heart racing, my lungs gasping for my next breath. I literally had to walk away, take a short break before I hyperventilated because <b>ALL WAS NOT WELL IN SECTOR 45!</b><br><br>After months and months of speculation and discussions, following every update and teaser on Twitter <b>NOTHING UNDER THE SUN</b> prepared me for how dark this book was going to be!<br><br>I felt my heart, each limb being slowly wrenched from my body!<br><br>Where do I even start?!<br><br>I've got to start with my heart – <b>Warner.</b><br><br>My poor, poor bae! My heart <b>BROKE</b>💔 for Warner.<br><br>Early on we find Warner dealing with some very dark, emotional stuff which includes coming to terms with the death of his farther. Warner's state of mind is such a complex, guttural, mind twisting rollercoaster of emotions. He doesn't regret his father's death but at the same time the void now left behind is one that Warner is desperately trying to figure out. Why does he care that the man who made his life a living hell and did everything to deny him an ounce of happiness is dead and gone? <br><br><i>I worry that my sadness will be interpreted as an endorsement of his choices—of his very existence—and in this matter I don’t want to be misunderstood, so I cannot admit that I grieve him, that I care at all for the loss of this monstrous man who raised me. And in the absence of healthy action I remain frozen, a sentient stone in the wake of my father’s death.</i><br><br>WHY, Tahereh! When will my Warner find peace?! <br><br>Warner is riddled with so much guilt, so much self loathing that he’s become paralyzed, so engrossed in his negativity that he prefers to dwell in his solitude where the demons he thought he'd somehow could control are beginning to control him. He’s mentally but most importantly emotionally closed himself off for the most part from the one person he treasures over all things in the universe, Juliette.<br><br>But as he battles this insidious darkness, he is most vulnerable when in Juliette's presence. His love for Juliette is unquestionably pure and so tangible… every precious second is like this beautiful love that you'd kill to keep safe. His heart belongs to her and I wanted him so badly to open up his soul fully to her! <br><br>But Warner’s old habits of keeping everything so close to the vest, his self defense mechanism to act unfazed or unaffected brings so much damage in its wake all I could do was suffer along as he took each step, barefoot over broken glass hoping to keep from losing the only bit of happiness he's ever had. <br><br>It pained me so much that he kept holding back to spare her, to spare himself pain… to ignore what shouldn't have been ignored. GAH!!!<br><br>Tahereh takes us deep into Warner's head and his POV had me glued to every word he spoke, every thought he had. We learn more about him and his past and I still want MORE!!!<br><br>I wholeheartedly believe Warner to be one of THE BEST written YA characters in YA lore. I LOVED that Tahereh didn't change his character into something or someone unrecognizable. He was still the Warner I had fallen in love with!<br><br><i>But I’ve been trying so hard to be a different man; to be, if not kinder, then at the very least, better. I don’t want to lose the love I’ve come to cherish.</i><br><br><b>Juliette</b> – I have to give Mafi a boat load of Kudos for how she handled Juliette's character. Although not the weak, deprecating, unsure girl we first met in book one, Juliette continues to struggle with her confidence level. Understandably so! She's only 17 and having taken control of the North American Sector of the Reestablishment she is overwhelmed by the tasks laid out before her as its new Supreme Commander – the responsibilities and expectations are overwhelming, threatening to choke her and extinguish her spark and hopes for a better world. But, in her efforts not too seem so needy and weak she fails to use the resources available to her, mainly Warner so she can gain the insight she desperately lacks to navigate this crazy, complicated new life that's her reality.<br><br><i> I hate how easily I fade in and out of confidence, how I waver between who I was and who I could be. My past still clings to me, skeleton hands holding me back even as I push forward into the light. And I can’t help but wonder how different I’d be today if I’d ever had someone to encourage me when I was growing up. I never had strong female role models.</i><br><br>Juliette discovers some MAJOR life altering revelations about herself, her past, her family. It drives her to shed the naïve girl, to kill the trusting person she wanted to be. The scene in Anderson's office brought me to tears! This was not the way things were supposed to turn out! <br><br>I was fretting that Juliette was on her way to becoming something harsh and unforgiving…a monster like Anderson. And the thought she had that she liked this new version better killed me!<br><br><i> For years my goal was to minimize myself—to fold and refold myself into a polygon of nothingness, to be too insignificant to be remembered. I wanted to appear innocent; I wanted to be thought of as quiet and harmless; I was worried always about how my very existence was terrifying to others and I did everything in my power to diminish myself, my light, my soul.<br><br>I wanted so desperately to placate the ignorant. I wanted so badly to appease the assholes who judged me without knowing me that I lost myself in the process.<br>But now? <br>Now, I laugh. Out loud. <br>Now, I don’t give a shit.</i><br><br><s>I am not insane</s><br><br>Well...I think <b>I AM</b> definitely insane after all the BOMBS that were dropped on Juliette. The manipulation that none of us foresaw devastated me and by the end of the book…NO WORDS!!!! <br><br><b>Warnette</b> I can't even go there right now! <br><br>All I can imagine hearing Tahereh say if I could ask her WHYYYYYY???!!!…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451312099ra/17527084.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>KENJI</b> – So good to have him! He's like the best friend that's always there for you when everything in your life has gone to piss. You can hold on to him and you just know he has your back. <br><br>I was happy to learn more about Kenji's past and having re-read the first half of this series this gave me a more rounded out appreciation for him. <br><br>He still is Kenji in every aspect that I've come to love but seeing his growing relationship with Warner was the best! There is still a mutual dislike for each other but at the same time Kenji is so there in his ever loving crude manner for Warner. Loved every scene these two shared.<br><br><i>“Uh-huh.” Kenji lifts an eyebrow. “So if, like, tomorrow she hooks up with some other dude you’re just gonna shrug and be like—I don’t know? Shake the guy’s hand? Take the happy couple out to dinner? Seriously?”</i><br><br>I'm also interested to see how his budding attraction to Nazeera turns out. I'm not calling this a ship yet but I would love to see these two together.<br><br><b>Castle</b> – I wasn't expecting to get this much of Castle but the skeletons that he uncovers just knocked me on my butt! His role went from mildly inconsequential to freaking critical! <b>THE SECRETS</b> this guy held blew my mind!!! <br><br><i> “Mr. Warner,” he says. “What do you think is going to happen when the truth of her past is finally revealed to her? Do you think she will accept it quietly? Calmly?”</i><br><br><b>CALMLY? I'M NOT CALM! DO YOU HEAR ME, CASTLE!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476639814ra/20865625.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Adam</b> – The lack of Adam was fairly surprising. I had expected more interaction between him and Juliette/Warner but I was fine with the dose I got. I was glad we finally got to learn what that secret convo between he and Warner was and that rooftop scene was amazing.<br><br>Adam is dealing with some daddy issues as well and I'm glad we got some background on his past and a bit into why things went so sour between he and Juliette.<br>Don't get me wrong, I still don't like Adam especially after his reaction to the state of Warnette's relationship. And I'm unsure how deeply I trust him. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497642587ra/23045892.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am ecstatic about the new characters introduced to begin this second trilogy! Such exciting characters I'm itching to know more about! <br><br>I wish I could predict where Tahereh is taking this story! Only she knows but this series is now on a totally different level of awesome I can surely predict this…<br><br>HOLD. ON!!!<br><br>Because after THAT ending?!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529793747ra/25843972.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>HIGHLY, HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!!!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9269977774519295155" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="sam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53964123-sam"><img alt="sam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603604230p2/53964123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1983077460?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="sam" href="/user/show/53964123-sam">sam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53964123-sam?shelf=dystopia-read">dystopia-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983077460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9932806017207136209"><b> Rating:</b>4.5 ⭐<br/><br/>What. The. Hell. I'm pretty sure if you've read this book already then you know exactly what I'm talking about. Every single time I thought something was going well in this book or tried to figure what was going on, I was proven horribly wrong.<br/><br/>What you will not expect: pretty much all of the plot twists. Well actually pretty much everything.<br/>What you will get: tahereh mafi playing with your emotions and hurting you in places you never knew existed.<br/>What I did: sat and stared at the wa</span>
  <span id="freeText9932806017207136209" style="display:none"><b> Rating:</b>4.5 ⭐<br /><br />What. The. Hell. I'm pretty sure if you've read this book already then you know exactly what I'm talking about. Every single time I thought something was going well in this book or tried to figure what was going on, I was proven horribly wrong.<br /><br />What you will not expect: pretty much all of the plot twists. Well actually pretty much everything.<br />What you will get: tahereh mafi playing with your emotions and hurting you in places you never knew existed.<br />What I did: sat and stared at the wall for an hour trying to figure out what I'm gonna do with my life.<br /><br />I've been waiting to read this book ever since it was announced that <i> Shatter Me </i> would no longer be a trilogy but a full fledged series with 6 books. Frankly, I've been dying to get back into this world and check up on my faves [Warner and Kenji 😀]. But, by reading the first couple of chapters itself, I knew there was no way in hell that this book wouldn't end badly for almost all of the characters. I'm not gonna tell you if I was right or wrong but if you wanna know then read the book!<br /><br />In this book Juliette tries to navigate her new life as the new Supreme Commander with Warner to guide her..kind of. This second half of the series is so dark and though I wasn't a huge fan of Juliette in the first three books, this newfound personality of her's is very mysterious and alluring. Its also so dark that after you read the first 3 books and then pick this one up, your jaw is sure to drop. I also liked the fact that this book was in dual perspectives (Warner's and Juliette's) and we get to know things about them that haven't even been hinted at in the other books. To be honest, I enjoyed Warner's perspective more than Juliette's. Overall, this was a very enthralling read that had me second guessing till the very end.<br /><br /> As long buried secrets are uncovered, one thing is for sure- the Reestablishment is not one to contend with.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9932806017207136209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UNCuu32eGOGpCNSoX6FL1r1gAdHndT3tDkpiJ1qg/4SCwkxaXRhfbte0zFppoiIjlhSgoajLi5s50cK0ZCG8Vw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V1KfHUsWG/piB0gN5xYpdPcdCBKbGLmY3YCoyXSvpByFQH38a5BcdRy7UP/RFUCB3GmpYtSmD+7qGwhaSi7nzw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText7717936990570880319" style="display:none">Tahereh Mafi is the <i>New York Times</i> and <i>USA Today</i> bestselling author of the <i>Shatter Me</i> series. She can usually be found over-caffeinated and stuck in a book. <i>Shatter Me</i> is her first series, with television rights optioned by ABC Signature Studios; <i>Furthermore</i>, her first middle grade novel, is on shelves now, and <i>Whichwood</i>, its darker companion, will be on shelves November 14, 2017.</span>
